           <table role="presentation" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:238px;margin-bottom:0;margin-top:0;background:#eee">
            <tbody>
             <tr>
              <td style="border:0;width:45px;height:45px;background:#ddd;text-align:center;font-size:14pt;font-weight:bold;color:black;padding:0 1px 0 0;line-height:1.25em;vertical-align:middle"><span class="noprint plainlinks purgelink"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=purge"><span title="Purge this page"><img alt="View-refresh.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/View-refresh.svg/45px-View-refresh.svg.png" decoding="async" width="45" height="45" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/View-refresh.svg/68px-View-refresh.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/View-refresh.svg/90px-View-refresh.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="48" data-file-height="48"></span></a></span></td>
              <td style="border:0;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;padding:0 4px 0 4px;height:45px;line-height:1.25em;color:black;vertical-align:middle"><span class="noprint plainlinks purgelink"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=purge"><span title="Purge this page">Click here to purge this page<br><font size="-2">(For help, see </font></span></a><font size="-2"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Purge" title="Wikipedia:Purge">Wikipedia:Purge</a>)</font></span></td>
             </tr>
            </tbody>
           </table>
          </div>This <b>Conflict of interest/Noticeboard</b> (<b>COIN</b>) page is for determining whether a specific editor has a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest" title="Wikipedia:Conflict of interest">conflict of interest</a> (COI) for a specific article and whether an edit by a COIN-declared COI editor does not meet a requirement of the Conflict of Interest guideline. A conflict of interest may occur when an editor has a close personal or business connections with article topics. An edit by a COIN-declared COI editor may not meet a requirement of the COI guideline when the edit advances outside interests more than it advances the aims of Wikipedia. Post here if you are concerned that an editor has a COI, and is using Wikipedia to promote their own interests at the expense of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NPOV" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:NPOV">neutrality</a>. For content disputes, try proposing changes at the article talk page first and otherwise follow the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Dispute_resolution" title="Wikipedia:Dispute resolution">Wikipedia:Dispute resolution</a> procedural policy. </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="3">
          <center>
           <center style="padding:5px 20px 5px 20px;border:solid 1px red; width:70%;">
            <span style="color: red;"><b>You <u>must</u> notify any editor who is the subject of a discussion. You may use <span class="nowrap"><code>{{<a href="/wiki/Template:Coin-notice" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Coin-notice">subst:coin-notice</a>}} ~~~~</code></span> to do so.</b></span>
           </center>
          </center> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="3"> 
          <hr> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="3"><b>Additional notes:</b> 
          <ul>
           <li>This page should only be used when ordinary talk page discussion has been attempted and failed to resolve the issue, such as when an editor has repeatedly added problematic material over an extended period.</li> 
           <li>Be careful not to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:OUTING" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:OUTING">out</a> other editors by posting personal information here. Wikipedia's <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:HARASS" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:HARASS">policy against harassment</a> takes precedence over the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:COI" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:COI">COI guideline</a>. If private information is needed to resolve COI editing, and if the issue is serious enough to warrant it, editors can email <span class="nowrap">paid-en-wp<img alt="@" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/At_sign.svg/15px-At_sign.svg.png" decoding="async" title="@" width="15" height="15" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/At_sign.svg/23px-At_sign.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/At_sign.svg/30px-At_sign.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="145" data-file-height="145">wikipedia.org</span> with the evidence, or <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Functionaries#Mailing_list" title="Wikipedia:Functionaries">email any functionary</a> for advice. <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:FUNCTIONARY" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:FUNCTIONARY">Functionaries</a> and members of the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:ARBCOM" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:ARBCOM">Arbitration Committee</a> will review private evidence and take any necessary action.</li> 
           <li>The COI guideline does not absolutely prohibit people with a connection to a subject from editing articles on that subject. Editors who have such a connection can still comply with the COI guideline by discussing proposed article changes first, or by making uncontroversial edits. COI allegations should not be used as a "trump card" in disputes over article content. However, <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PAID" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:PAID">paid editing without disclosure</a> is prohibited. Consider using the template series {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Uw-paid1" title="Template:Uw-paid1">Uw-paid1</a>}} through {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Uw-paid4" title="Template:Uw-paid4">Uw-paid4</a>}}.</li> 
           <li>Your report or advice request regarding COI incidents should include <a href="/wiki/Help:Diff#Linking_to_a_diff" title="Help:Diff">diff links</a> and focus on one or more items in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:COI" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:COI">COI guideline</a>. In response, COIN may determine whether a specific editor has a COI for a specific article. There are three possible outcomes to your COIN request:</li>
          </ul> 
          <dl>
           <dd>
            <dl>
             <dd>
              1. COIN consensus determines that an editor has a COI for a specific article. In response, the relevant article talk pages may be tagged with {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Connected_contributor" title="Template:Connected contributor">Connected contributor</a>}}, the article page may be tagged with {{<a href="/wiki/Template:COI" title="Template:COI">COI</a>}}, and/or the user may be warned via {{subst:<a href="/wiki/Template:Uw-coi" title="Template:Uw-coi">uw-coi|Article</a>}}.
             </dd> 
             <dd>
              2. COIN consensus determines that an editor does not have a COI for a specific article. In response, editors should refrain from further accusing that editor of having a conflict of interest. Feel free to repost at COIN if additional COI evidence comes to light that was not previously addressed.
             </dd> 
             <dd>
              3. There is no COIN consensus. Here, <a href="/wiki/User:Lowercase_sigmabot_III" title="User:Lowercase sigmabot III">Lowercase sigmabot III</a> will automatically archive the thread when it is older than 14 days.
             </dd>
            </dl>
           </dd>
          </dl> 
          <ul>
           <li>Once COIN declares that an editor has a COI for a specific article, COIN (or a variety of other noticeboards) may be used to determine whether an edit by a COIN-declared COI editor does not meet a requirement of the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest" title="Wikipedia:Conflict of interest">Wikipedia:Conflict of interest</a> guideline.</li>
          </ul> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td colspan="3"> 
          <table width="100%"> 
           <tbody>
            <tr> 
             <td style="width: 50%; font-size: 115%; vertical-align: top;">
              <div role="navigation" class="navbox" aria-labelledby="Are_you_in_the_right_place?" style="border:2px ridge #CAE1FF;;padding:3px">
               <table class="nowraplinks mw-collapsible mw-collapsed navbox-inner" style="border-spacing:0;background:transparent;color:inherit">
                <tbody>
                 <tr>
                  <th scope="col" class="navbox-title" colspan="2" style="background-color:#AAD1FF;">
                   <div id="Are_you_in_the_right_place?" style="font-size:114%;margin:0 4em">
                    Are you in the right place?
                   </div></th>
                 </tr>
                 <tr>
                  <td colspan="2" class="navbox-list navbox-odd vlist" style="width:100%;padding:0px;text-align: left;">
                   <div style="padding:0em 0.25em"> 
                    <ul>
                     <li>An editor can be biased without additionally having a COI. Issues involving bias may be more suited to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Neutral_point_of_view/Noticeboard" title="Wikipedia:Neutral point of view/Noticeboard">Wikipedia:Neutral point of view/Noticeboard</a>.</li> 
                     <li>Issues involving the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Biographies_of_living_persons" title="Wikipedia:Biographies of living persons">biographies of living persons policy</a> (BLP) may be more suited to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Biographies_of_living_persons/Noticeboard" title="Wikipedia:Biographies of living persons/Noticeboard">Wikipedia:Biographies of living persons/Noticeboard</a>.</li> 
                     <li>Commercial <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Username_policy" title="Wikipedia:Username policy">usernames</a> should be reported to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Usernames_for_administrator_attention" title="Wikipedia:Usernames for administrator attention">Wikipedia:Usernames for administrator attention</a>.</li> 
                     <li>Obvious cases of <b><a href="https://lists.wikimedia.org/pipermail/wikien-l/2006-September/054719.html" class="extiw" title="mailarchive:wikien-l/2006-September/054719.html">corporate vanity</a></b> can be tagged with {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Db-spam" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Db-spam">db-spam</a>}}.</li> 
                     <li>Articles written about a person, group, club or band by such a person, group, club or band with <b>no assertion of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Notability" title="Wikipedia:Notability">notability</a></b> can be tagged with {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Db-bio" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Db-bio">db-bio</a>}} instead.</li> 
                     <li>This page is <b>not</b> for reporting simple <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Vandalism" title="Wikipedia:Vandalism">vandalism</a>, material that can easily be fixed or removed without argument, or non-conflict of interest breaches of the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Neutral_point_of_view" title="Wikipedia:Neutral point of view">neutral point of view</a> policy.</li>
                    </ul> 
                   </div></td>
                 </tr>
                </tbody>
               </table>
              </div> </td> 
             <td style="width: 50%; font-size: 115%; vertical-align: top;">
              <div role="navigation" class="navbox" aria-labelledby="Notes_for_volunteers" style="border:2px ridge #CAE1FF;;padding:3px">
               <table class="nowraplinks mw-collapsible mw-collapsed navbox-inner" style="border-spacing:0;background:transparent;color:inherit">
                <tbody>
                 <tr>
                  <th scope="col" class="navbox-title" colspan="2" style="background-color:#AAD1FF;">
                   <div id="Notes_for_volunteers" style="font-size:114%;margin:0 4em">
                    Notes for volunteers
                   </div></th>
                 </tr>
                 <tr>
                  <td colspan="2" class="navbox-list navbox-odd vlist" style="width:100%;padding:0px;text-align: left;">
                   <div style="padding:0em 0.25em"> 
                    <dl>
                     <dt>
                      To close a report
                     </dt>
                    </dl> 
                    <ul>
                     <li>Add <a href="/wiki/Template:Resolved" title="Template:Resolved">Template:Resolved</a> at the head of the complaint, with the reason for closing and your signature.</li> 
                     <li>Old issues are taken away by the archive bot.</li>
                    </ul> 
                    <dl>
                     <dt>
                      Other ways to help
                     </dt>
                    </dl> 
                    <ul>
                     <li>All editors are encouraged to help resolve reports of COI editing. More problematic articles can be found in <a href="/wiki/Category:Wikipedia_articles_with_possible_conflicts_of_interest" title="Category:Wikipedia articles with possible conflicts of interest">Category:Wikipedia articles with possible conflicts of interest</a>.</li> 
                     <li>A list of possible <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Autobiography" title="Wikipedia:Autobiography">autobiographies</a> found by <a href="/wiki/User:AlexNewArtBot" title="User:AlexNewArtBot">bot</a>. This is the large mechanically-generated list of articles having a suspected COI that used to be shown here in full. You are still invited to peruse the list and, if you have an opinion on whether it's a real COI, edit that file directly. When you see a case in that list that needs input from other editors, you may want to create a regular noticeboard entry for it, below.<i></i></li> 
                     <li><a href="/wiki/Category:Wikipedia_requested_edits" title="Category:Wikipedia requested edits">Category:Wikipedia requested edits</a>. Editors who believe they have a conflict of interest may ask someone else to make edits for them. Please visit this category and respond to one of these requests. Whether you perform it or not, you should undo the {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Request_edit" title="Template:Request edit">Request edit</a>}} when you are done to remove the article from the category. Leave a Talk comment for the requester to explain your decision.</li>
                    </ul> 
                   </div></td>
                 </tr>
                </tbody>
               </table>
              </div> </td>
            </tr>
           </tbody>
          </table> </td>

       <li><span class="plainlinks userlinks"><span class="userlinks-username"><a href="/w/index.php?title=User:165.127.111.20&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:165.127.111.20 (page does not exist)">165.127.111.20</a></span> <span class="plainlinks">(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:165.127.111.20" title="User talk:165.127.111.20">talk</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/165.127.111.20" title="Special:Contributions/165.127.111.20">contribs</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:DeletedContributions/165.127.111.20" title="Special:DeletedContributions/165.127.111.20">deleted contribs</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;user=165.127.111.20">logs</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:AbuseLog&amp;wpSearchUser=165.127.111.20">edit filter log</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Block/165.127.111.20" title="Special:Block/165.127.111.20">block user</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=block&amp;page=User:165.127.111.20">block log</a>)</span></span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>These are IP user registered to a State of Colorado government computers, likely in the legislative offices in most cases and perhaps some others. The user contributions logs (especially from the .14. block) include several edits to various Colorado politicians, which is almost certainly one or more undisclosed COIs. I <i>would</i> propose banning the addresses from editing anything having to do with Colorado politics, but as it's an IP user it seems difficult to enforce a selective ban. There are likely other IP addresses involved as well, and also probably more pages, but I have not identified them yet. <i>In addition, many if not most of these pages also have edits from named/IP users with potential COIs, which likely could be investigated further by looking at other users who edit from these IP eddresses.</i> Frankly, the more I look at these pages the more I find with regards to implicated users and articles. I would consider a blanket ban on IP edits from this IP block if possible, and further investigation. - - <b><a href="/wiki/User:Mathmitch7" title="User:Mathmitch7">mathmitch7</a></b> <sup>(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Mathmitch7" title="User talk:Mathmitch7">talk</a>/<a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Mathmitch7" title="Special:Contributions/Mathmitch7">contribs</a>)</sup> 14:49, 13 May 2021 (UTC) </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        And what is with <a href="/w/index.php?title=Template:Infobox_Colorado_Legislation&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Template:Infobox Colorado Legislation (page does not exist)">Template:Infobox Colorado Legislation</a>? The only other US states that seem to have similar templates are used on articles <i>for actual pieces of legislation</i>. (see <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/Template:Infobox_Oklahoma_legislation%7C">here for example</a>). Adding these to a stack of politician's articles looks like promotion to me, listing their achievements by detailing every bill they have sponsored - that seems the kind of content that belongs on their own websites or on the legislature's website, not in an encyclopedia. <a href="/wiki/User:Melcous" title="User:Melcous">Melcous</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Melcous" title="User talk:Melcous">talk</a>) 05:51, 14 May 2021 (UTC)

      <ul>
       <li><span><a href="/wiki/Cleanaway" title="Cleanaway">Cleanaway</a>&nbsp;<span class="plainlinks lx">(<a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Cleanaway" title="Special:EditPage/Cleanaway">edit</a> | <a href="/wiki/Talk:Cleanaway" title="Talk:Cleanaway">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:PageHistory/Cleanaway" title="Special:PageHistory/Cleanaway">history</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/Cleanaway" title="Special:WhatLinksHere/Cleanaway">links</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Cleanaway&amp;action=watch">watch</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special%3ALog&amp;page=Cleanaway">logs</a>)</span></span></li>

       <li><span class="plainlinks userlinks"><span class="userlinks-username"><a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Mags1984&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Mags1984 (page does not exist)">Mags1984</a></span> <span class="plainlinks">(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Mags1984" title="User talk:Mags1984">talk</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Mags1984" title="Special:Contributions/Mags1984">contribs</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:DeletedContributions/Mags1984" title="Special:DeletedContributions/Mags1984">deleted contribs</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;user=Mags1984">logs</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:AbuseLog&amp;wpSearchUser=Mags1984">edit filter log</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Block/Mags1984" title="Special:Block/Mags1984">block user</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=block&amp;page=User:Mags1984">block log</a>)</span></span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>I'm highly suspicious that this is an undisclosed paid editor. The username appears to be a shortened form of "Cleanaway Content". Example edits such as <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Cleanaway&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=957512335">this one</a> and <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Cleanaway&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=1023076594">this one</a> are highly suspect. They even state openly in an edit summary that the edit was undertaken based on <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Cleanaway&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=968573966">Cleanaway's investor advice</a>. The account has been editing since 2018 and has only ever edited <a href="/wiki/Cleanaway" title="Cleanaway">Cleanaway</a>. Reviewing the edit history it would appear as though Cleanaway have employed somebody to monitor their article here. <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/92.24.246.11" title="Special:Contributions/92.24.246.11">92.24.246.11</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:92.24.246.11" title="User talk:92.24.246.11">talk</a>) 11:12, 14 May 2021 (UTC) </p>
      <p>P-blocked from Cleanaway to see if we can get their attention. No objection to anyone unblocking them once they've agreed to disclose and stop directly editing, but the username may also be problematic. <a href="/wiki/User:Valereee" title="User:Valereee">valereee</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Valereee" title="User talk:Valereee">talk</a>) 14:10, 14 May 2021 (UTC) </p>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tony_Hawks">Tony Hawks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Tony Hawks">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <ul>
       <li><span><a href="/wiki/Tony_Hawks" title="Tony Hawks">Tony Hawks</a>&nbsp;<span class="plainlinks lx">(<a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Tony_Hawks" title="Special:EditPage/Tony Hawks">edit</a> | <a href="/wiki/Talk:Tony_Hawks" title="Talk:Tony Hawks">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:PageHistory/Tony_Hawks" title="Special:PageHistory/Tony Hawks">history</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/Tony_Hawks" title="Special:WhatLinksHere/Tony Hawks">links</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Tony_Hawks&amp;action=watch">watch</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special%3ALog&amp;page=Tony+Hawks">logs</a>)</span></span></li> 
       <li><span class="plainlinks userlinks"><span class="userlinks-username"><a href="/wiki/User:Cliffsmith23" title="User:Cliffsmith23">Cliffsmith23</a></span> <span class="plainlinks">(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Cliffsmith23" title="User talk:Cliffsmith23">talk</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Cliffsmith23" title="Special:Contributions/Cliffsmith23">contribs</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:DeletedContributions/Cliffsmith23" title="Special:DeletedContributions/Cliffsmith23">deleted contribs</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;user=Cliffsmith23">logs</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:AbuseLog&amp;wpSearchUser=Cliffsmith23">edit filter log</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Block/Cliffsmith23" title="Special:Block/Cliffsmith23">block user</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=block&amp;page=User:Cliffsmith23">block log</a>)</span></span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>I know the British comedian Tony Hawks as a casual acquaintance in my local pub, and we've chatted occasionally. A few months ago (pre-lockdown) we were talking about Wikipedia, and he mentioned that his page had a very old and low-quality photo, and that it showed the wrong date of birth. I told him that I had an editing account, and that I'd be happy to update his details. This clearly wasn't a matter of urgency, since his PA has only just sent me an email today with a new photo and his correct DOB. In the interests of making Wikipedia more factually accurate, I've edited his page with these new details, but a much more experienced editor has given me a warning about a possible COI. I'd like to make it very clear that I do not work for Tony in any capacity, I have not been paid, nor do I expect to be paid, for making this edit, and Tony will only benefit from it to the extent that he'll probably get birthday cards on the right date from now on. I'm not very experienced at editing Wikipedia, so I hope I haven't committed a major faux pas here, but my intentions were pure. <a href="/wiki/User:Cliffsmith23" title="User:Cliffsmith23">Cliffsmith23</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Cliffsmith23" title="User talk:Cliffsmith23">talk</a>) 19:27, 17 May 2021 (UTC) </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <span class="template-ping">@<a href="/wiki/User:Cliffsmith23" title="User:Cliffsmith23">Cliffsmith23</a>:</span> Thanks for your forthright honesty. This does not strike me as a big deal, especially since you have taken the time to write the above. Please use the talk page to request edits in future, and include sources with the request. You could tell Tony and his agent that advice as well. Thanks. <a href="/wiki/User:Possibly" title="User:Possibly">--- Possibly</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Possibly" title="User talk:Possibly">talk</a>) 05:49, 18 May 2021 (UTC)

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Aidong_Zhang">Aidong Zhang</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Aidong Zhang">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p><a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Aidongzhang&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Aidongzhang (page does not exist)">Aidongzhang</a>&nbsp;(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Aidongzhang" title="User talk:Aidongzhang">talk</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Aidongzhang" title="Special:Contributions/Aidongzhang">contribs</a>), who I believe to be the same person as <a href="/wiki/Aidong_Zhang" title="Aidong Zhang">Aidong Zhang</a>, has initiated <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:BLPREQDEL" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:BLPREQDEL">WP:BLPREQDEL</a> deletion proceedings against the article, as is her right. However, after repeatedly being told not to directly edit the article and being pointed to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AUTOBIO" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:AUTOBIO">WP:AUTOBIO</a>, she also refuses to stop editing the article directly (<a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/1023875265" title="Special:Diff/1023875265">diff on my talk</a>). I believe this needs to be enforced with a targeted block (or, if that fails to work, semiprotection) but I am too <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:INVOLVED" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:INVOLVED">WP:INVOLVED</a> to do it myself, so I am bringing it here with that request. Will notify. <a href="/wiki/User:David_Eppstein" title="User:David Eppstein">David Eppstein</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:David_Eppstein" title="User talk:David Eppstein">talk</a>) 21:09, 18 May 2021 (UTC) </p>

It's quite curious.<a href="/wiki/User:Possibly" title="User:Possibly">--- Possibly</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Possibly" title="User talk:Possibly">talk</a>) 21:23, 18 May 2021 (UTC)

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sarabod99_and_MoMA_promotion">Sarabod99 and MoMA promotion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Sarabod99 and MoMA promotion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <ul>
       <li><span class="plainlinks userlinks"><span class="userlinks-username"><a href="/wiki/User:Sarabod99" title="User:Sarabod99">Sarabod99</a></span> <span class="plainlinks">(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Sarabod99" title="User talk:Sarabod99">talk</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Sarabod99" title="Special:Contributions/Sarabod99">contribs</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:DeletedContributions/Sarabod99" title="Special:DeletedContributions/Sarabod99">deleted contribs</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;user=Sarabod99">logs</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:AbuseLog&amp;wpSearchUser=Sarabod99">edit filter log</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Block/Sarabod99" title="Special:Block/Sarabod99">block user</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=block&amp;page=User:Sarabod99">block log</a>)</span></span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>User Sarabod99 is apparently <a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Grants:Project/Rapid/Sara_Bodinson/MoMA_Art_%2B_Feminism_Edit-a-thon_2020">an employee of MoMA</a>' and has been adding MoMA projects and links to articles for several years. The recent addition of external links in batches (like <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Sekou_Cooke&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=1024530074">this</a> and <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=J._Yolande_Daniels&amp;type=revision&amp;diff=1024519067&amp;oldid=1021624411">this</a> and <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=V._Mitch_McEwen&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=1024528087">this</a> and <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Walter_J._Hood&amp;diff=prev&amp;oldid=1024523782">this</a> and <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Walter_J._Hood&amp;diff=next&amp;oldid=1024513442">this</a> and <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=V._Mitch_McEwen&amp;type=revision&amp;diff=1024528087&amp;oldid=1023347865">this</a>, which added a the MoMA youtube, MoMA Coursera course, MoMA magazine and MoMA calendar) isn't cool. No response on talk page; I rolled back one set of links and had it reverted by Sarabod99. They have continued to add links despite reverts and talk page messages. All that's needed here is a proper talk page disclosure, and a commitment to be a lot more sparing and judicious when adding MoMA info. Pinging <span class="template-ping">@<a href="/wiki/User:Theredproject" title="User:Theredproject">Theredproject</a>:</span> as they would likely be able to help. <a href="/wiki/User:Possibly" title="User:Possibly">--- Possibly</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Possibly" title="User talk:Possibly">talk</a>) 18:18, 22 May 2021 (UTC) </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <a href="/wiki/User:Possibly" title="User:Possibly">Possibly</a>, They may be busy. There's an edit-a-thon today: <a class="external free" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Meetup/Black_Lunch_Table/MoMA_blackness_architecture_2021">https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Meetup/Black_Lunch_Table/MoMA_blackness_architecture_2021</a> <a href="/wiki/User:Vexations" title="User:Vexations">Vexations</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Vexations" title="User talk:Vexations">talk</a>) 18:39, 22 May 2021 (UTC)

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Rick_Roeber">Rick Roeber</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Rick Roeber">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <ul>
       <li><span><a href="/wiki/Rick_Roeber" title="Rick Roeber">Rick Roeber</a>&nbsp;<span class="plainlinks lx">(<a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Rick_Roeber" title="Special:EditPage/Rick Roeber">edit</a> | <a href="/wiki/Talk:Rick_Roeber" title="Talk:Rick Roeber">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:PageHistory/Rick_Roeber" title="Special:PageHistory/Rick Roeber">history</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/Rick_Roeber" title="Special:WhatLinksHere/Rick Roeber">links</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Rick_Roeber&amp;action=watch">watch</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special%3ALog&amp;page=Rick+Roeber">logs</a>)</span></span></li> 
       <li><span class="plainlinks userlinks"><span class="userlinks-username"><a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Barefootrick&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Barefootrick (page does not exist)">Barefootrick</a></span> <span class="plainlinks">(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Barefootrick" title="User talk:Barefootrick">talk</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Barefootrick" title="Special:Contributions/Barefootrick">contribs</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:DeletedContributions/Barefootrick" title="Special:DeletedContributions/Barefootrick">deleted contribs</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;user=Barefootrick">logs</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:AbuseLog&amp;wpSearchUser=Barefootrick">edit filter log</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Block/Barefootrick" title="Special:Block/Barefootrick">block user</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=block&amp;page=User:Barefootrick">block log</a>)</span></span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>I strongly believe there has been undisclosed paid editing at the page <a href="/wiki/Rick_Roeber" title="Rick Roeber">Rick Roeber</a> by the user <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Barefootrick&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Barefootrick (page does not exist)">Barefootrick</a>. The most obvious way I know this is because of this edit summary: <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Rick_Roeber&amp;diff=765701169&amp;oldid=">[1]</a></span> For over a decade now <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Lee%27s_Summit,_Missouri&amp;diff=164733996&amp;oldid=">[2]</a></span>, this user has inserted content promoting Roeber into articles, including <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:REFSPAM" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:REFSPAM">WP:REFSPAM</a> of links to Roeber's website into the external links section of <a href="/wiki/Barefoot_running" title="Barefoot running">Barefoot running</a>: <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Barefoot_running&amp;diff=166735348&amp;oldid=">[3]</a></span> Most notably, this user's recent edits were to remove content regarding a child sex abuse allegation against Roeber which recently led to him being expelled from the Missouri House of Representatives: <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Rick_Roeber&amp;diff=987268565&amp;oldid=">[4]</a></span> <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Rick_Roeber&amp;diff=987268884&amp;oldid=">[5]</a></span> <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Rick_Roeber&amp;diff=991028172&amp;oldid=">[6]</a></span> <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Rick_Roeber&amp;diff=993643143&amp;oldid=">[7]</a></span> <span class="plainlinks"><a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Rick_Roeber&amp;diff=995735843&amp;oldid=">[8]</a></span> Please look into this and block if necessary. Thank you. <a href="/wiki/User:AllegedlyHuman" title="User:AllegedlyHuman">AllegedlyHuman</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:AllegedlyHuman" title="User talk:AllegedlyHuman">talk</a>) 04:16, 23 May 2021 (UTC) </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <span class="template-ping">@<a href="/wiki/User:AllegedlyHuman" title="User:AllegedlyHuman">AllegedlyHuman</a>:</span> is Hatersandbullies the same user on Rick Roeber? <a href="/wiki/User:Possibly" title="User:Possibly">--- Possibly</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Possibly" title="User talk:Possibly">talk</a>) 07:50, 23 May 2021 (UTC)

Or you could ask for a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PBLOCK" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:PBLOCK">pBlock</a>, seeing as the only thing they are doing here is apparently COI editing. The cited edit summary, "I don't want my age listed", does not imply paid editing, but autobiography. <a href="/wiki/User:Possibly" title="User:Possibly">--- Possibly</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Possibly" title="User talk:Possibly">talk</a>) 08:21, 23 May 2021 (UTC)

      <p>This (likely UPE) sockfarm was focused on adding negative coverage (sometimes BLP violations) about certain Kuwaiti people and organizations. <a href="/wiki/User:MarioGom" title="User:MarioGom">MarioGom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:MarioGom" title="User talk:MarioGom">talk</a>) 13:51, 23 May 2021 (UTC) </p>

       <dd>
        Note that I didn't go in-depth on all of their edits. Apparently their edits to some of the subjects are positive POV. So each article and contribution should be reviewed in context. <a href="/wiki/User:MarioGom" title="User:MarioGom">MarioGom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:MarioGom" title="User talk:MarioGom">talk</a>) 14:07, 23 May 2021 (UTC)

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Centre_for_Chinese_Contemporary_Art">Centre for Chinese Contemporary Art</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Centre for Chinese Contemporary Art">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <ul>
       <li><span><a href="/wiki/Centre_for_Chinese_Contemporary_Art" title="Centre for Chinese Contemporary Art">Centre for Chinese Contemporary Art</a>&nbsp;<span class="plainlinks lx">(<a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Centre_for_Chinese_Contemporary_Art" title="Special:EditPage/Centre for Chinese Contemporary Art">edit</a> | <a href="/wiki/Talk:Centre_for_Chinese_Contemporary_Art" title="Talk:Centre for Chinese Contemporary Art">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:PageHistory/Centre_for_Chinese_Contemporary_Art" title="Special:PageHistory/Centre for Chinese Contemporary Art">history</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/Centre_for_Chinese_Contemporary_Art" title="Special:WhatLinksHere/Centre for Chinese Contemporary Art">links</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Centre_for_Chinese_Contemporary_Art&amp;action=watch">watch</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special%3ALog&amp;page=Centre+for+Chinese+Contemporary+Art">logs</a>)</span></span></li> 
       <li><span class="plainlinks userlinks"><span class="userlinks-username"><a href="/wiki/User:K8tmoon" title="User:K8tmoon">K8tmoon</a></span> <span class="plainlinks">(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:K8tmoon" title="User talk:K8tmoon">talk</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/K8tmoon" title="Special:Contributions/K8tmoon">contribs</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:DeletedContributions/K8tmoon" title="Special:DeletedContributions/K8tmoon">deleted contribs</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;user=K8tmoon">logs</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:AbuseLog&amp;wpSearchUser=K8tmoon">edit filter log</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Block/K8tmoon" title="Special:Block/K8tmoon">block user</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=block&amp;page=User:K8tmoon">block log</a>)</span></span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>I first came to this article to update it, as many of the sources cited in it are self-published. Whilst researching the subject, I found information that leads me to think that the primary editor of the article named above is closely related to the subject, and maybe a senior employee at the organisation. The user has no disclosed conflicts of interest, and I have raised the issue on their user talk page. The user has denied any COI. I noticed that over several years most of their edits appear to be on BLPs with a connection to the Center for Chinese Contemporary Art. The user's edits also predominantly rely on self-published sources by the subject of the article, and they have declared in the article talk pages, that they had the intention of removing information which was considered critical or negative, in favour of information from self-published sources. The article has previously and remains tagged for containing promotional material. </p>
      <p>I also took a look at other articles that the user has edited, as they have been a long-time editor. Other edits, for example to the article for the <a href="/wiki/Institute_For_Education" title="Institute For Education">Institute For Education</a>, were also predominantly to list notable members of staff. I have found information which leads me to think that when these edits were made, they were also an employee of the subject of this article. Their user page indicates that they are an archivist by profession. There is a publically available online profile that matches the educational background declared on the user page and that also details close links to the subjects of many of the other articles listed by the user as created or significantly edited - granted, it may be a coincidence but seems unlikely. I cannot share any details from this without the danger of outing. Can this be investigated? --<a href="/wiki/User:ArchivesandLetters" title="User:ArchivesandLetters">ArchivesandLetters</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:ArchivesandLetters" title="User talk:ArchivesandLetters">talk</a>) 22:43, 23 May 2021 (UTC) </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <dl>
         <dd>
          <a href="/wiki/User:Possibly" title="User:Possibly">--- Possibly</a> What do we do if the user in question does not respond? Can we assume a COI and tag the article? I can work on addressing the issues in the article and make a note on the talk pages in case others want to help.<a href="/wiki/User:ArchivesandLetters" title="User:ArchivesandLetters">ArchivesandLetters</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:ArchivesandLetters" title="User talk:ArchivesandLetters">talk</a>) 15:47, 26 May 2021 (UTC)
         </dd>
        </dl>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <dl>
         <dd>
          <dl>
           <dd>
            I was unaware of current COI guidance until it was flagged up by <a href="/wiki/User:ArchivesandLetters" title="User:ArchivesandLetters">ArchivesandLetters</a> on my user page. I have now made adjustments to my user page following guidance for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:COIADVICE" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:COIADVICE"> Making uncontroversial edits</a> and current advice for editors who work in the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GLAM/Getting_started" title="Wikipedia:GLAM/Getting started">GLAM sector</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CURATOR" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:CURATOR"> cultural sector</a>. At the time this post was made on this page I had stated that I have never been a paid advocate, but I was taking time to familiarize myself with current guidance on COI before I felt I could fully respond. I have now responded to the request on my user page and confirmed that I do have a conflict of interest &amp; I will now stick to the guidelines mentioned above. <a href="/wiki/User:K8tmoon" title="User:K8tmoon">K8tmoon</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:K8tmoon" title="User talk:K8tmoon">talk</a>) 21:54, 26 May 2021 (UTC) 
            <dl>
             <dd>
              Yes, so to sum up, after two editors asked repeatedly, and after one denial, K8tmoon admits to being based at the Centre for Chinese Contemporary Art. Not really the way to generate trust. <a href="/wiki/User:Possibly" title="User:Possibly">--- Possibly</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Possibly" title="User talk:Possibly">talk</a>) 22:05, 26 May 2021 (UTC) 
              <dl>
               <dd>
                Good summary @<a href="/wiki/User:Possibly" title="User:Possibly">Possibly</a>. I must say that whilst I do support the principle that experts <b>should</b> contribute their knowledge and resources to Wikipedia, I cannot support a claim that editors in the GLAM sector can freely edit articles about either their employers or their own organisations. @<a href="/wiki/User:K8tmoon" title="User:K8tmoon">K8tmoon</a>'s edits over the last 3 years appear to have primarily been on the article about their organisation, or associates who have previously worked there. Most edits to BLPs were simply to add the fact that they had previously worked at the Centre for Chinese Contemporary Art. There are few edits from what I can see which have contributed specialist knowledge beyond promoting the organisation. @<a href="/wiki/User:K8tmoon" title="User:K8tmoon">K8tmoon</a> if your edits are part of the work you do as a paid member of the organisation, then I think this constitutes paid editing. I see you have also removed the article from your list of significantly edited articles. <a href="/wiki/User:ArchivesandLetters" title="User:ArchivesandLetters">ArchivesandLetters</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:ArchivesandLetters" title="User talk:ArchivesandLetters">talk</a>) 23:27, 26 May 2021 (UTC)
               </dd>
              </dl>
             </dd> 
             <dd>
              I realised that my previous comment may be misunderstood. All the edits I have made to Wikipedia have not been as part of the work I do as a paid member of staff of the organisations I have worked for. Therefore I believe I have never been a paid advocate as I have never received anything for my Wikipedia edits. Now being aware of current COI guidelines, I will modify my Wikipedia contributions in future. I did not deny that I work for the Centre, I only stated that I have never been paid to edit Wikipedia. I only edit Wikipedia in my spare time as a hobby.<a href="/wiki/User:K8tmoon" title="User:K8tmoon">K8tmoon</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:K8tmoon" title="User talk:K8tmoon">talk</a>) 08:33, 29 May 2021 (UTC)
             </dd>
            </dl>
           </dd>

      <p>Hello, i have found an editor who is doing coi work. At first the editor moved the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Dibyojyoti_Dutta&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Dibyojyoti Dutta (page does not exist)">Dibyojyoti Dutta</a> to <a href="/w/index.php?title=Annwesha_Hazra&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Annwesha Hazra (page does not exist)">Annwesha Hazra</a> (see here <a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Special:MobileDiff/1024313281">[10]</a>). Then the editor tried the article in different name(see here <a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Annwesha_Hazra">[12]</a>) and when I saw the subject was written like a CV/Advert then I tagged the article with CV and ADVERT and after checking the history of the user's talk page i added a tag COI and the user removed the tag. So I must say he/she has COI in this article <a href="/w/index.php?title=Annwesha_Hazra&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Annwesha Hazra (page does not exist)">Annwesha Hazra</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:TryingToDo" title="User:TryingToDo">Bengal Boy</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:TryingToDo" title="User talk:TryingToDo">talk</a>) 05:48, 24 May 2021 (UTC) </p>

      <p><a href="/wiki/User:Mynameisparitoshmandal" title="User:Mynameisparitoshmandal">Mynameisparitoshmandal</a>: the disclosure looks good. There's no furhter problem with that. Please, do read carefully all relevant guides related to paid editing. You can start here: <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PAY" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:PAY">WP:PAY</a>. There's a few things you did here, such as adding a {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Pp" title="Template:Pp">pp</a>}} template (<a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/1024612340" title="Special:Diff/1024612340">diff</a>), removing maintenance templates (<a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/1024806674" title="Special:Diff/1024806674">diff</a>), removing comments by other editors (<a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/1024810742" title="Special:Diff/1024810742">diff</a>) or by-passing the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:AFC" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:AFC">Articles for Creation</a> process for a previously declined draft, that taken together with your paid status can easily get you blocked. So you really need to back off, read <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:PAY" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:PAY">WP:PAY</a> and act more carefully. <a href="/wiki/User:MarioGom" title="User:MarioGom">MarioGom</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:MarioGom" title="User talk:MarioGom">talk</a>) 08:18, 24 May 2021 (UTC) </p>

      <h2><span id="not_your_usual_COI_issue.2C_and_not_for_the_faint_of_heart"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="not_your_usual_COI_issue,_and_not_for_the_faint_of_heart">not your usual COI issue, and not for the faint of heart</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: not your usual COI issue, and not for the faint of heart">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <ul>
       <li><span id="Zoophilia"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/Zoophilia" title="Zoophilia">Zoophilia</a> (<a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Zoophilia&amp;action=edit">edit</a>&nbsp;| <a href="/wiki/Talk:Zoophilia" title="Talk:Zoophilia">talk</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Zoophilia&amp;action=history">history</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Zoophilia&amp;action=protect">protect</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Zoophilia&amp;action=delete">delete</a></span>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Zoophilia&amp;limit=999">links</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Zoophilia&amp;action=watch">watch</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Zoophilia">logs</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/pageviews?pages=Zoophilia&amp;project=en.wikipedia.org">views</a>)</span></li> 
       <li><span id="History_of_zoophilia"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/wiki/History_of_zoophilia" title="History of zoophilia">History of zoophilia</a> (<a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=History_of_zoophilia&amp;action=edit">edit</a>&nbsp;| <a href="/wiki/Talk:History_of_zoophilia" title="Talk:History of zoophilia">talk</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=History_of_zoophilia&amp;action=history">history</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=History_of_zoophilia&amp;action=protect">protect</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=History_of_zoophilia&amp;action=delete">delete</a></span>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/History_of_zoophilia&amp;limit=999">links</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=History_of_zoophilia&amp;action=watch">watch</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=History+of+zoophilia">logs</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/pageviews?pages=History_of_zoophilia&amp;project=en.wikipedia.org">views</a>)</span></li> 
       <li><span id="Legality_of_bestiality_by_country_or_territory"></span><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion lx"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Legality_of_bestiality_by_country_or_territory&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Legality of bestiality by country or territory (page does not exist)">Legality of bestiality by country or territory</a> (<a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Legality_of_bestiality_by_country_or_territory&amp;action=edit">edit</a>&nbsp;| <a href="/w/index.php?title=Talk:Legality_of_bestiality_by_country_or_territory&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Talk:Legality of bestiality by country or territory (page does not exist)">talk</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Legality_of_bestiality_by_country_or_territory&amp;action=history">history</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Legality_of_bestiality_by_country_or_territory&amp;action=protect">protect</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Legality_of_bestiality_by_country_or_territory&amp;action=delete">delete</a></span>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Whatlinkshere/Legality_of_bestiality_by_country_or_territory&amp;limit=999">links</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Legality_of_bestiality_by_country_or_territory&amp;action=watch">watch</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;page=Legality+of+bestiality+by+country+or+territory">logs</a>&nbsp;| <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/pageviews?pages=Legality_of_bestiality_by_country_or_territory&amp;project=en.wikipedia.org">views</a>)</span> (currently at AFD and probably on it's way out but the page history may provide some insight)</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>For those that may not be familiar with the term, "zoophilia" was/is commonly known as bestiality, so yes, we're talking about humans having sex with animals. My concern here is that there is an observable pattern across these articles that seems to be attempts to normalize such activities and/or to suggest they are explicitly legal in certain places, when in actuality whoever wrote the material is either interpreting the law for themselves, mis-characterizing the content of the source material, or basing it on questionable sources. One editor is asking fellow "enthusiasts" on Twitter to help them with sourcing certain claims regarding the legality of having sex with animals in Germany. I won't share the link per <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:OUTING" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:OUTING">WP:OUTING</a> but it's pretty obviously the same person. So, my concern is that our coverage of animal rape is being influenced by people who think raping animals is pretty great. More attention from people who don't feel that way might be helpful in bringing this content into line with Wikipedia standards. <a href="/wiki/User:Beeblebrox" title="User:Beeblebrox">Beeblebrox</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Beeblebrox" title="User talk:Beeblebrox">talk</a>) 22:21, 30 May 2021 (UTC) </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <s>The situation you have described is not a conflict of interest. Gay men and lesbians might be be motivated to edit our articles about <a href="/wiki/Homosexuality" title="Homosexuality">homosexuality</a>, <a href="/wiki/History_of_homosexuality" title="History of homosexuality">history of homosexuality</a> and <a href="/wiki/LGBT_rights_by_country_or_territory" title="LGBT rights by country or territory">LGBT rights by country or territory</a>. No one would consider that a conflict of interest. <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Zetablocker&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Zetablocker (page does not exist)">Zetablocker</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Zetablocker" title="User talk:Zetablocker">talk</a>) 21:51, 31 May 2021 (UTC)</s> <span style="font-size:85%;">Zetablocker blocked as <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NOTHERE" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:NOTHERE">NOTHERE</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:GorillaWarfare" title="User:GorillaWarfare">GorillaWarfare</a>&nbsp;(she/her&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="/wiki/User_talk:GorillaWarfare" title="User talk:GorillaWarfare">talk</a>) 23:02, 31 May 2021 (UTC)</span> 
        <dl>
         <dd>
          No, that's a strawman, the correct parallel would be <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CHILDPROTECT" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:CHILDPROTECT">WP:CHILDPROTECT</a>. We don't tolerate advocacy of abuse. <b><span style="font-family: Arial;"><a href="/wiki/User:Acroterion" title="User:Acroterion"><span style="color: black;">Acroterion</span></a> <small><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Acroterion" title="User talk:Acroterion"><span style="color: gray;">(talk)</span></a></small></span></b> 22:09, 31 May 2021 (UTC)
         </dd> 
         <dd>
          Bank robbers might be motivated to edit articles about bank robbery for that matter. The simple facts of the matter are that bestiality is ether explicitly illegal, or considered morally repugnant, almost everywhere, but some who have edited such content in the past have seen fit to use Wikipedia to promote a viewpoint suggesting otherwise. And done so in a manner entirely incompatible with multiple Wikipedia policies, to the extent that at least one of the articles listed above is best described as a work of fiction, in my opinion. And I think that comparisons with LGBT issues are dubious for multiple reasons, and should be avoided. <a href="/wiki/User:AndyTheGrump" title="User:AndyTheGrump">AndyTheGrump</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:AndyTheGrump" title="User talk:AndyTheGrump">talk</a>) 22:12, 31 May 2021 (UTC) 
          <dl>
           <dd>
            <s>There is a clear parallel between how LGBT people have been treated in the past and how zoophiles are treated now. It is possible to edit articles about your sexuality without having a conflict of interest. It is possible to discuss the merits of articles without insulting the people referred to by the article. <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Zetablocker&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Zetablocker (page does not exist)">Zetablocker</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Zetablocker" title="User talk:Zetablocker">talk</a>) 22:36, 31 May 2021 (UTC)</s> <span style="font-size:85%;">Zetablocker blocked as <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NOTHERE" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:NOTHERE">NOTHERE</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:GorillaWarfare" title="User:GorillaWarfare">GorillaWarfare</a>&nbsp;(she/her&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="/wiki/User_talk:GorillaWarfare" title="User talk:GorillaWarfare">talk</a>) 23:02, 31 May 2021 (UTC)</span>
           </dd>
          </dl>
         </dd>
        </dl>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <ul>
       <li>I really can't express how infuriating the "it's just like being gay" argument is, but that's another issue. I realize this is not what COIN is normally for but I don't think we have a "advocacy for illegal abusive sexual practices" noticeboard. The obvious attack sock above was kind enough to go straight to ANI though, (hence the block) so some more eyes may be on the topic because of that. <a href="/wiki/User:Beeblebrox" title="User:Beeblebrox">Beeblebrox</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Beeblebrox" title="User talk:Beeblebrox">talk</a>) 01:10, 1 June 2021 (UTC)</li>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Conflict_of_interest_editing">Conflict of interest editing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Conflict of interest editing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <ul>
       <li><span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Soludo_Marcel&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Soludo Marcel (page does not exist)">Soludo Marcel</a>&nbsp;<span class="plainlinks lx">(<a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Soludo_Marcel" title="Special:EditPage/Soludo Marcel">edit</a> | <a href="/w/index.php?title=Talk:Soludo_Marcel&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Talk:Soludo Marcel (page does not exist)">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:PageHistory/Soludo_Marcel" title="Special:PageHistory/Soludo Marcel">history</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/Soludo_Marcel" title="Special:WhatLinksHere/Soludo Marcel">links</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Soludo_Marcel&amp;action=watch">watch</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special%3ALog&amp;page=Soludo+Marcel">logs</a>)</span></span></li> 
       <li><span class="plainlinks userlinks"><span class="userlinks-username"><a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Horizonlove&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Horizonlove (page does not exist)">Horizonlove</a></span> <span class="plainlinks">(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Horizonlove" title="User talk:Horizonlove">talk</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Horizonlove" title="Special:Contributions/Horizonlove">contribs</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:DeletedContributions/Horizonlove" title="Special:DeletedContributions/Horizonlove">deleted contribs</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;user=Horizonlove">logs</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:AbuseLog&amp;wpSearchUser=Horizonlove">edit filter log</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Block/Horizonlove" title="Special:Block/Horizonlove">block user</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=block&amp;page=User:Horizonlove">block log</a>)</span></span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>Conflict of interest editing whereby the article creator had the photo on the article as their own work but did not disclose a COI. Furthermore they have displayed a battle ground behavior by removing relevant warning templates pertaining UPE and has thus far exhibited an <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:IDHT" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:IDHT">WP:IDHT</a> attitude. Furthermore the subject of the article is possibly the worst non notable article Ive this year. The creator of the article has also been engaging in <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:REFACTOR" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:REFACTOR">refactoring</a> comments made by other users. As an anti-spam editor that I am, I can affirm that this is undisclosed paid editing. <b><a href="/wiki/User:Celestina007" title="User:Celestina007">Celestina007</a></b> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Celestina007" title="User talk:Celestina007">talk</a>) 00:39, 31 May 2021 (UTC) </p>

      <h2><span id="How_do_I_declare_CoI_from_5_years_ago.3F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="How_do_I_declare_CoI_from_5_years_ago?">How do I declare CoI from 5 years ago?</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: How do I declare CoI from 5 years ago?">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <ul>
       <li><span><a href="/wiki/GSM_Cell_ID" title="GSM Cell ID">GSM Cell ID</a>&nbsp;<span class="plainlinks lx">(<a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/GSM_Cell_ID" title="Special:EditPage/GSM Cell ID">edit</a> | <a href="/wiki/Talk:GSM_Cell_ID" title="Talk:GSM Cell ID">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:PageHistory/GSM_Cell_ID" title="Special:PageHistory/GSM Cell ID">history</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/GSM_Cell_ID" title="Special:WhatLinksHere/GSM Cell ID">links</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=GSM_Cell_ID&amp;action=watch">watch</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special%3ALog&amp;page=GSM+Cell+ID">logs</a>)</span></span></li> 
       <li><span><a href="/wiki/OpenCellID" title="OpenCellID">OpenCellID</a>&nbsp;<span class="plainlinks lx">(<a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/OpenCellID" title="Special:EditPage/OpenCellID">edit</a> | <a href="/wiki/Talk:OpenCellID" title="Talk:OpenCellID">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:PageHistory/OpenCellID" title="Special:PageHistory/OpenCellID">history</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/OpenCellID" title="Special:WhatLinksHere/OpenCellID">links</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=OpenCellID&amp;action=watch">watch</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special%3ALog&amp;page=OpenCellID">logs</a>)</span></span></li> 
       <li><span class="plainlinks userlinks"><span class="userlinks-username"><a href="/wiki/User:DaxServer" title="User:DaxServer">DaxServer</a></span> <span class="plainlinks">(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:DaxServer" title="User talk:DaxServer">talk</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/DaxServer" title="Special:Contributions/DaxServer">contribs</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:DeletedContributions/DaxServer" title="Special:DeletedContributions/DaxServer">deleted contribs</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;user=DaxServer">logs</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:AbuseLog&amp;wpSearchUser=DaxServer">edit filter log</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Block/DaxServer" title="Special:Block/DaxServer">block user</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=block&amp;page=User:DaxServer">block log</a>)</span></span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>I'd like to know how I can disclose CoI edits that I have made about 5 years ago. During my work at a former employer, Unwired Labs, I have edited the articles: <a href="/wiki/GSM_Cell_ID" title="GSM Cell ID">GSM Cell ID</a> and <a href="/wiki/OpenCellID" title="OpenCellID">OpenCellID</a>. I'm not aware of edits to other articles at the moment, but history might reveal some. I have not actively received any payments for my edits, apart from the monthly salary for my work at the company. However, edits to Wikipedia is not part of my job resposibilities. The article <a href="/wiki/GSM_Cell_ID" title="GSM Cell ID">GSM Cell ID</a> was used for promotional purposes, to the best of my knowledge during my work. I could not comment on further advancements after I parted in November 2017. </p>
      <p>I was not aware of the CoI requirements in the early days. As I progressed over time, I learnt more and has thus mostly refrained from editing. I might have edited, but couldn't recall. I have added <code>{{Update}}</code> (<a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/786780889" title="Special:Diff/786780889">Special:Diff/786780889</a>) and <code>{{Advert}}</code> (<a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/800745380" title="Special:Diff/800745380">Special:Diff/800745380</a>) templates to <a href="/wiki/OpenCellID" title="OpenCellID">OpenCellID</a> and <code>{{Primary sources}}</code> (<a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/788141583" title="Special:Diff/788141583">Special:Diff/788141583</a>) to <a href="/wiki/GSM_Cell_ID" title="GSM Cell ID">GSM Cell ID</a>, for which I was reprimanded. In 2020, when I knew better, I have noted the CoI in the edit summary (<a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/961037277" title="Special:Diff/961037277">Special:Diff/961037277</a>) as per policy. </p>
      <p>What are the next steps that I should follow? <a href="/wiki/User:DaxServer" title="User:DaxServer">-- DaxServer</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:DaxServer" title="User talk:DaxServer">talk</a>) 17:27, 31 May 2021 (UTC) </p>

      <p>Editor Dr. Universe seems to have created the page <a href="/w/index.php?title=Nikesh_S._Dattani&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Nikesh S. Dattani (page does not exist)">Nikesh S. Dattani</a> sometime before 2014. It was deleted in 2014 (deletion discussion <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Nikesh_S._Dattani" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Nikesh S. Dattani">here</a>). They recreated the page under a different name of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Nike_Dattani&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Nike Dattani (page does not exist)">Nike Dattani</a> somewhat later; the different name had the effect of avoiding a swift G4. It was recently deleted (2nd deletion discussion <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Nike_Dattani" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Nike Dattani">here</a>). </p>
      <p>In addition to the persistent efforts at a biography page for Dattani (with possible attempt to evade G4), the editor has added prominent mention of Dattani to a large number of pages, and has resisted attempts by other editors to remove these. The pages above all include prominent, and I believe in most cases <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:UNDUE" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:UNDUE">WP:UNDUE</a>, mention of Dattani. Indeed, it would be surprising if a scientist for whom AfD regulars saw little sign of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NPROF" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:NPROF">WP:NPROF</a> notability had contributed so substantially to 10 different problems. Diffs of particular concern is: </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/1025647647" title="Special:Diff/1025647647">Partial reversion of content-removal by AfD closer</a> at <a href="/wiki/Timeline_of_quantum_computing_and_communication" title="Timeline of quantum computing and communication">Timeline of quantum computing and communication</a></li> 
       <li>At <a href="/wiki/Hierarchical_equations_of_motion" title="Hierarchical equations of motion">Hierarchical equations of motion</a>, Dr. Universe added prominent coverage of Dattani in <a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/860045377" title="Special:Diff/860045377">Special:Diff/860045377</a>, <a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/860048178" title="Special:Diff/860048178">Special:Diff/860048178</a>. An edit war then seems to have ensued (with other editors that, it should be said, did appear to have an opposing COI) - see <a href="/wiki/Talk:Hierarchical_equations_of_motion" title="Talk:Hierarchical equations of motion">Talk:Hierarchical equations of motion</a>.</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>There seems to be a larger pattern of adding prominent coverage of Dattani, sometimes while removing other references. Examples from Dr. Universe include <a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/800349616" title="Special:Diff/800349616">Special:Diff/800349616</a>, <a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/657025573" title="Special:Diff/657025573">Special:Diff/657025573</a>, creation and promotion of Dattani on <a href="/wiki/Morse/Long-range_potential" title="Morse/Long-range potential">Morse/Long-range potential</a>, creation of page and unbalanced mention of Dattani at <a href="/wiki/Robert_J._LeRoy" title="Robert J. LeRoy">Robert J. LeRoy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/746821298" title="Special:Diff/746821298">Special:Diff/746821298</a>, <a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/617019234" title="Special:Diff/617019234">Special:Diff/617019234</a>, likely others. IP editors have also added references to Dattani (with the appearance of promotion), including <a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/921951064" title="Special:Diff/921951064">Special:Diff/921951064</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Special:Diff/910596971" title="Special:Diff/910596971">series of diffs beginning here</a>. Some of these may even be <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:DUE" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:DUE">WP:DUE</a>, and most of the edits are not independently so problematic; I find the pattern concerning. </p>
      <p>The editor disclosed, or appeared to disclose, some form of COI in the 2nd <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Nike_Dattani" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Nike Dattani">article for deletion discussion</a> (where several editors expressed COI concerns), but the disclosure seemed to misunderstand the nature of COI on Wikipedia. I am not comfortable unilaterally adding connected contributor tags, and I'm not sure that it would help. The editor has a 10+ year history at Wikipedia, with a bit over 1000 edits in their history, some of which are helpful and positive. Edits to these pages where I have COI concerns do comprise a significant portion of their edits - already, their 48 (!!) edits at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Articles_for_deletion/Nike_Dattani" title="Wikipedia:Articles for deletion/Nike Dattani">WP:Articles for deletion/Nike Dattani</a> make up around 4% of their publicly visible edit history. This sure looks to me like a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:DUCK" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:DUCK">WP:DUCK</a> with a conflict of interest. </p>
      <p>I am bringing this to COIN now following a <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Russ_Woodroofe#MLR" title="User talk:Russ Woodroofe">particularly unhelpful discussion</a> on my talk page. I think this needs eyes other than my own. </p>
      <p>I had <a href="/wiki/User_talk:XOR%27easter#Morse_potential" title="User talk:XOR'easter">earlier asked</a> <a href="/wiki/User:XOR%27easter" title="User:XOR'easter">XOR'easter</a> for an opinion (as a physics expert) on the <a href="/wiki/Morse/Long-range_potential" title="Morse/Long-range potential">Morse/Long-range potential</a> article, which I was uncertain justified a standalone article. I will also leave a note at Wikiproject physics, as some expertise may be helpful in untangling the situation. <a href="/wiki/User:Russ_Woodroofe" title="User:Russ Woodroofe">Russ Woodroofe</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Russ_Woodroofe" title="User talk:Russ Woodroofe">talk</a>) 11:35, 1 June 2021 (UTC) </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <span class="template-ping">@<a href="/wiki/User:Russ_Woodroofe" title="User:Russ Woodroofe">Russ Woodroofe</a>:</span> Well spotted. <b><span style="text-shadow:7px 7px 8px black; font-family:Papyrus"><a href="/wiki/User:Scope_creep" title="User:Scope creep"><span style="color:#3399ff">scope_creep</span></a><sup><a href="/wiki/User_talk:Scope_creep#top" title="User talk:Scope creep">Talk</a></sup></span></b> 11:53, 1 June 2021 (UTC) 
        <dl>
         <dd>
          Subject of the discussion replying here: 
          <ul>
           <li>Even though I've had an account for 13 years, this concept of a "noticeboard" is very new to me, as is much of the terminology being used here. I find this extremely overwhelming.</li> 
           <li>The top says "This page should only be used when ordinary talk page discussion has been attempted and failed to resolve the issue, such as when an editor has repeatedly added problematic material over an extended period." Russ only replied to me <b>once</b> on his talk page, and did not reply to my response to that reply. Even though it looks like my response was much longer, Russ had done a few other things in between which I found to be very harmful, so I wanted to address those things too. <i>I would very much appreciate if we can try to resolve this on a talk page first</i>.</li> 
           <li>Russ has accused me of re-creating an article "with possible attempt to evade G4", but that is extremely deceiving, and Russ knows that because in the recent AfD discussion, an admin already investigated the difference between the 2014 article and the 2018 one, and determined that they were substantially different. Russ said the second article was created "somewhat later" even though it was <b>4 years</b> later and was a totally different article (as an admin already determined). Russ was thorough when it worked against me, but vague by saying "somewhat later" when it could make it look like I violated some rule about G4 (which I'd never heard of before, by the way!).</li> 
           <li>There has been no basis given for the claim of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:UNDUE" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:UNDUE">WP:UNDUE</a> mentions (though I just learned that term recently from Russ, and I still have to read up on it), and it seems like Russ Woodroofe taking revenge against me for suggesting that he made undue mentions of <a href="/wiki/Michael_Woodroofe" title="Michael Woodroofe">Michael Woodroofe</a> (an article created by Russ Woodroofe).</li> 
           <li>"Partial reversion of content-removal by AfD closer at Timeline of quantum computing and communication" is I think an unfair characterization of what happened. The AfD closer removed the "[[ ]]" around all mentions of the deleted article so that the text would appear in ordinary black rather than a red hyperlink, but on only <b>one out of 14 articles</b> that she did this, she removed more than just the hyperlink and removed substantially more. I thought this was a mistake because it was only done in 1/14 articles, and it wasn't even done properly (the first part of a sentence was removed, but the part containing the reference was not, so the article looked bizarre with a lone reference floating around). Furthermore, "quantum computing" is not a topic for which the admin was an expert, so removing an entire entry from "Timeline for Quantum Computing" seemed to be an "overly" bold move, especially since they only removed "[[ ]]" from the other 13 articles (not removal of the entire sentence). <b>When Russ reverted my reversion, I left it at that, and didn't touch it anymore, even though I did think the removal of an entire entry from the timeline was a bit extreme</b>.</li> 
           <li>It's true that in 2018 I added to the Hierarchical Equations of Motion article, mention of the person I wrote a biography (which also by the way was in 2018). But that article has changed a lot since then, and I'm happy with the article remaining as it is with minimal mentioning of the person I wrote the biography about. I think the last thing I did was change "Wilkins" to "Wilkins and Dattani" because the citation was to a 2-author paper published in Journal of Computational and Theoretical Chemistry.</li>
