I remember correcting that typo and thinking it wouldn't be a big deal because people already know that I'm not the subject, I'm just being accused of being too closely connected to the subject. It's extremely easy to prove the former (although the initial ways I can think of, like me showing a picture of my ID or something, would I hope not be necessary if we respect the rules about WP:OUTING that I just learned from Russ's comment). My use of a Waterloo IP was something that I did not need to say here, and I was worried that by saying that people would try to use it against me, but I thought that since I don't know the subject personally or have professional ties with them, there would be no harm in being open and honest about it, plus there's 60,000 members of UWaterloo at any given time, and millions of alumni and even more when we include visitors and members of the public since it's a public university funded by tax-payers who are allowed to spend time there without being a member. I'm finding a lot of this to be intimidating and I don't think it's fair to say I broke WP rules based on me using a Waterloo IP (which you first of all learned directly from me, in this specific discussion: I didn't have to tell it to you but I didn't know people would try to use each piece of information against me that way... this is making me nervous about being open in the future, which is unfortunate because all this time I thought were were supposed to be welcoming and not making others feel uncomfortable in this way... I feel "guilty until proven innocent" and that the burden of proof for everything is on the defendant rather than the accuser). After learning from Russ just now about WP:OUTING, I don't feel comfortable having <i>comments</i> from years ago, which were clearly not even complete since the sentence ended abruptly without finishing, used to make assumptions about me, and I worry that the follow-up questions and responses to my answers did push me to want to just say my name and show my ID so that we could settle all this once-and-for-all, but I don't think we're supposed to be made to feel like we're forced to "OUT" ourselves.

The last post prior to yours seems to have been made on May 24, and 14 days hasn't passed since that day. Now, unfortunately, it appears that your post (and subsequently this response made by me) has probably reset the clock, which means that the thread will be archived 14 days from today as long as nobody posts anything further. There's really no rush to archive discussions; most of the time they just end naturally when people stop posting and thus will eventually be archived at some point (if automatic archiving has been set up). If they're not archived exactly after 14 days have passed, then it's not really a big deal; moreover, if the thread is formally <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:CLOSE" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:CLOSE">closed</a> before 14 days have passed, then it might even be archived a little sooner (which again isn't a big deal). -- <a href="/wiki/User:Marchjuly" title="User:Marchjuly">Marchjuly</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Marchjuly" title="User talk:Marchjuly">talk</a>) 01:20, 3 June 2021 (UTC)

      <h2><span id="B.E1.BA.A3o_.C4.90.E1.BA.A1i"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="B?o_??i">B?o ??i</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: B?o ??i">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <ul>
       <li><span><a href="/wiki/B%E1%BA%A3o_%C4%90%E1%BA%A1i" title="B?o ??i">B?o ??i</a>&nbsp;<span class="plainlinks lx">(<a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/B%E1%BA%A3o_%C4%90%E1%BA%A1i" title="Special:EditPage/B?o ??i">edit</a> | <a href="/wiki/Talk:B%E1%BA%A3o_%C4%90%E1%BA%A1i" title="Talk:B?o ??i">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:PageHistory/B%E1%BA%A3o_%C4%90%E1%BA%A1i" title="Special:PageHistory/B?o ??i">history</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/B%E1%BA%A3o_%C4%90%E1%BA%A1i" title="Special:WhatLinksHere/B?o ??i">links</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=B%E1%BA%A3o_%C4%90%E1%BA%A1i&amp;action=watch">watch</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special%3ALog&amp;page=B%E1%BA%A3o+%C4%90%E1%BA%A1i">logs</a>)</span></span></li> 
       <li><span class="plainlinks userlinks"><span class="userlinks-username"><a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Royal_Vietnam&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Royal Vietnam (page does not exist)">Royal Vietnam</a></span> <span class="plainlinks">(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Royal_Vietnam" title="User talk:Royal Vietnam">talk</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Royal_Vietnam" title="Special:Contributions/Royal Vietnam">contribs</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:DeletedContributions/Royal_Vietnam" title="Special:DeletedContributions/Royal Vietnam">deleted contribs</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;user=Royal+Vietnam">logs</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:AbuseLog&amp;wpSearchUser=Royal+Vietnam">edit filter log</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Block/Royal_Vietnam" title="Special:Block/Royal Vietnam">block user</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=block&amp;page=User:Royal+Vietnam">block log</a>)</span></span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>Single-purpose account seems to be self inserting themselves into this article. After wack-a-moleing unreferenced edits they have provided a new edit which references a book written by the user in question. I am not sure if this is vandalism or a conflict of interest. However they clearly seem to be the self proclaimed "pretender to the throne" that they keep editing into the article without any third party sources. <a href="/wiki/User:Spongie555" title="User:Spongie555">Spongie555</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Spongie555" title="User talk:Spongie555">talk</a>) 05:30, 3 June 2021 (UTC) </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="An_unusual_COIN_report">An unusual COIN report</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: An unusual COIN report">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>Normally, I show up here to discuss someone with a conflict of interest who isn'y following the rules. Today I have someone who <b>is</b> following the rules and is getting nowhere. </p>
      <p>I often assist COI editors who follow the rules. I look at their suggested edits and either implement they or ask that they be made less promotional, etc. </p>
      <p>Usually, nobody has a problem with this. At <a href="/wiki/Talk:NowMedical#Requested_changes_from_NowMedical" title="Talk:NowMedical">Talk:NowMedical#Requested changes from NowMedical</a> there was a disagreement about whether my edits were good, and I decided to withdraw because I am unwilling to get into a dispute over this. </p>
      <p>Alas, that left the COI editor, who really seems to want to follow our rules -- hanging. </p>
      <p>Could I please request some other editors to look at the situation and offer an opinion as to whether my edits were appropriate and should be made? I like them and think they were good, but then again, I like everything I do and always agree with my own opinions.&nbsp;:) --<a href="/wiki/User:Guy_Macon" title="User:Guy Macon">Guy Macon</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Guy_Macon" title="User talk:Guy Macon">talk</a>) 19:37, 3 June 2021 (UTC) </p>

       <dd>

It seems like a content dispute. Perhaps using the {{<a href="/wiki/Template:Requestedit" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Requestedit">requestedit</a>}} template would bring a wider range of opinions?<a href="/wiki/User:Possibly" title="User:Possibly">--- Possibly</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Possibly" title="User talk:Possibly">talk</a>) 19:46, 3 June 2021 (UTC)

This COIN report says that <a href="/wiki/User:Guy_Macon" title="User:Guy Macon">User:Guy Macon</a> wants to make edits but they were disagreed upon by the person who declared themselves as working for the company.         Just like Guy Macon, I dislike arguing about requested changes. The proper way for a coi editor is to present the information on the talk page, and let other people edit the article. If it becomes a matter of bargaining, I normally disengage. If I consider the end result unsatisfactory, I may edit the article as I would any other like the usual BRD editing by people without a coi. Those with a coi should stay out of the discussion. I am not happy with the present state of the article, but then I am generally not happy with criticisms sections ,which I think are better integrated. And this article has the additional problem thart we don't usually use consumer anecdotes, which can never be representative, but in this case it seems to be the clearest way to show the situation. I think on balance its OK as it is , in the Justlettersandnumbers version. <b><a href="/wiki/User:DGG" title="User:DGG"> DGG</a></b> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:DGG" title="User talk:DGG"> talk </a>) 01:24, 4 June 2021 (UTC)

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Omar_Al_Ashi">Omar Al Ashi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Omar Al Ashi">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <ul>
       <li><span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Grandiose_Digital_Media&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Grandiose Digital Media (page does not exist)">Grandiose Digital Media</a>&nbsp;<span class="plainlinks lx">(<a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Grandiose_Digital_Media" title="Special:EditPage/Grandiose Digital Media">edit</a> | <a href="/w/index.php?title=Talk:Grandiose_Digital_Media&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Talk:Grandiose Digital Media (page does not exist)">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:PageHistory/Grandiose_Digital_Media" title="Special:PageHistory/Grandiose Digital Media">history</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/Grandiose_Digital_Media" title="Special:WhatLinksHere/Grandiose Digital Media">links</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Grandiose_Digital_Media&amp;action=watch">watch</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special%3ALog&amp;page=Grandiose+Digital+Media">logs</a>)</span></span></li> 
       <li><span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Omar_Al_Ashi&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Omar Al Ashi (page does not exist)">Omar Al Ashi</a>&nbsp;<span class="plainlinks lx">(<a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Omar_Al_Ashi" title="Special:EditPage/Omar Al Ashi">edit</a> | <a href="/w/index.php?title=Talk:Omar_Al_Ashi&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Talk:Omar Al Ashi (page does not exist)">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:PageHistory/Omar_Al_Ashi" title="Special:PageHistory/Omar Al Ashi">history</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/Omar_Al_Ashi" title="Special:WhatLinksHere/Omar Al Ashi">links</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Omar_Al_Ashi&amp;action=watch">watch</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special%3ALog&amp;page=Omar+Al+Ashi">logs</a>)</span></span></li> 
       <li><span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jatin_Ahuja&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Jatin Ahuja (page does not exist)">Jatin Ahuja</a>&nbsp;<span class="plainlinks lx">(<a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Jatin_Ahuja" title="Special:EditPage/Jatin Ahuja">edit</a> | <a href="/w/index.php?title=Talk:Jatin_Ahuja&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Talk:Jatin Ahuja (page does not exist)">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:PageHistory/Jatin_Ahuja" title="Special:PageHistory/Jatin Ahuja">history</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/Jatin_Ahuja" title="Special:WhatLinksHere/Jatin Ahuja">links</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Jatin_Ahuja&amp;action=watch">watch</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special%3ALog&amp;page=Jatin+Ahuja">logs</a>)</span></span></li> 
       <li><span class="plainlinks userlinks"><span class="userlinks-username"><a href="/wiki/User:EdwardMill" title="User:EdwardMill">EdwardMill</a></span> <span class="plainlinks">(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:EdwardMill" title="User talk:EdwardMill">talk</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/EdwardMill" title="Special:Contributions/EdwardMill">contribs</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:DeletedContributions/EdwardMill" title="Special:DeletedContributions/EdwardMill">deleted contribs</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;user=EdwardMill">logs</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:AbuseLog&amp;wpSearchUser=EdwardMill">edit filter log</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Block/EdwardMill" title="Special:Block/EdwardMill">block user</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=block&amp;page=User:EdwardMill">block log</a>)</span></span></li> 
       <li>Weeks before EdwardMill joined, someone with the same name as the owner of Grandiose, <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Mhd_Huzaifa&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Mhd Huzaifa (page does not exist)">Mhd_Huzaifa</a> created a sandbox draft for Omar Al Ashi<a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/User:Mhd_Huzaifa/sandbox/Omar_Al_Ashi">[19]</a> and disclosed a COI. It is clear that Al-Ashi is a client of Grandiose as are several other articles they've added and links they've added. They also recreated <a href="/w/index.php?title=Jatin_Ahuja&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Jatin Ahuja (page does not exist)">Jatin Ahuja</a> which was a target of many paid spam socks. It's clear to me that EdwardMill is either an employee of Grandiose or a freelancer hired to do their dirty work. It's also worth noting that <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://grandiosedigitalmedia.com/social-media-marketing-and-verification-support/">Grandiose offers Wikipedia page creation</a> to their clients as well, and yet, mysteriously, we have no disclosures on-wiki of such editing. Further, according to <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.easternherald.com/2020/07/17/concierge-services-dubai-trend/">Grandiose's own press release on</a> <a class="external text" href="https://www.wikidata.org/wiki/Q107009899">Cristian Marano</a>, they are a client, which EdwardMill has conveniently created on Wikidata as is <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://richendtech.com/jorgedian-dihigo-caro-the-cuban-entrepreneur-enlightens-his-fans-with-his-interest-in-cars/">this</a> <a class="external text" href="https://www.wikidata.org/wiki/Q107008873">guy</a> who EM also created on Wikidata and lastly <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://chadmeihuizen.com/index.php/win-exciting-giveaways/">this</a>, another Grandiose client, also created <a class="external text" href="https://www.wikidata.org/wiki/Q106994433">on wd</a>This is an elaborate paid editing spam campaign. <a href="/wiki/User:Praxidicae" title="User:Praxidicae"><span style="color:#007FFF;font-size:11px">BEACHIDICAE?</span></a> 14:47, 4 June 2021 (UTC)</li>
      </ul> 
      <p>Dear Praxidicae, I respect your opinion. But the page created for Grandiose had been drafted before it went to Articles for Deletion page. I've been working for many other wikipedia profiles and did the best I could do from my side. As for Grandiose and its clients, the founder didn't pitch anything to me. It's just yes something I do not want to comment on. However, not all of them are their clients. I got to know about them through one of their employees who didn't pay anything to me as you mentioned "This is an elaborate paid editing spam campaign". I doubt your words and wholly deny what you said in the sentence. Even if Grandiose's employee had pitched to me, the simple reason to put them on Wikidata is because they are a notable entity as you can see. </p>
      <p>I would suggest that you please do not directly comment upon your decision on 2 articles that was published and think it of a mere decision made by the 'Wiki-notability guidelines'. </p>
      <p>I hope you understand what me as an editor is simply trying to say. </p>
      <p>Conclusion: 1. Yes, Grandiose Employee told them have some notable people that might be of your interest (NOTHING PROMOTIONAL) 2. I made my decision to put them on Wikipedia as a real entity (MY DECISION) 3. The pages got deleted, and I respect your comment (YOUR DECISION) </p>
      <p>Thank you <a href="/wiki/User:EdwardMill" title="User:EdwardMill">EdwardMill</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:EdwardMill" title="User talk:EdwardMill">talk</a>) 15:50, 4 June 2021 (UTC) </p>
      <p>If I wanted I could've created hundreds of pages in the due time. But I am strictly against 'PAID WORK' and more interested towards creating and editing content that should be done. I am not associated with anyone! <a href="/wiki/User:EdwardMill" title="User:EdwardMill">EdwardMill</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:EdwardMill" title="User talk:EdwardMill">talk</a>) 15:53, 4 June 2021 (UTC) </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <dl>
         <dd>
          Then how are the images of their clients your own work? And how is it that you managed to spam their clients - and only their clients crosswiki and yet have no relationship? <a href="/wiki/User:Praxidicae" title="User:Praxidicae"><span style="color:#007FFF;font-size:11px">BEACHIDICAE?</span></a> 16:04, 4 June 2021 (UTC)
         </dd>
        </dl>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <p>The thing about grandiose offering wikipedia page creation that was in here <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://grandiosedigitalmedia.com/social-media-marketing-and-verification-support/">Grandiose offers Wikipedia page creation</a> seems to be gone... <a href="/wiki/User:Kadermonkey" title="User:Kadermonkey">Kadermonkey</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Kadermonkey" title="User talk:Kadermonkey">talk</a>) 16:41, 4 June 2021 (UTC) </p>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Randy_Fine">Randy Fine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:Conflict_of_interest/Noticeboard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Randy Fine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <ul>
       <li><span><a href="/wiki/Randy_Fine" title="Randy Fine">Randy Fine</a>&nbsp;<span class="plainlinks lx">(<a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Randy_Fine" title="Special:EditPage/Randy Fine">edit</a> | <a href="/wiki/Talk:Randy_Fine" title="Talk:Randy Fine">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:PageHistory/Randy_Fine" title="Special:PageHistory/Randy Fine">history</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:WhatLinksHere/Randy_Fine" title="Special:WhatLinksHere/Randy Fine">links</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Randy_Fine&amp;action=watch">watch</a> | <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special%3ALog&amp;page=Randy+Fine">logs</a>)</span></span></li> 
       <li><span class="plainlinks userlinks"><span class="userlinks-username"><a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Floridagopman&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Floridagopman (page does not exist)">Floridagopman</a></span> <span class="plainlinks">(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Floridagopman" title="User talk:Floridagopman">talk</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Floridagopman" title="Special:Contributions/Floridagopman">contribs</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:DeletedContributions/Floridagopman" title="Special:DeletedContributions/Floridagopman">deleted contribs</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;user=Floridagopman">logs</a>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:AbuseLog&amp;wpSearchUser=Floridagopman">edit filter log</a><span class="sysop-show">&nbsp;<b></b> <a href="/wiki/Special:Block/Floridagopman" title="Special:Block/Floridagopman">block user</a></span>&nbsp;<b></b> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Log&amp;type=block&amp;page=User:Floridagopman">block log</a>)</span></span></li>
      </ul> 
      <p><a href="/wiki/Randy_Fine" title="Randy Fine">Randy Fine</a> has a page, who is is a Republican politician in the Florida House of Representatives. A user with the name <span class="template-ping">@<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Floridagopman&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Floridagopman (page does not exist)">Floridagopman</a>:</span> (Which seems like Randy Fine himself because the name has Florida and initials GOP is synonymous with the Republican Party) has made many changes to page. Glancing at the edits, this user has removed many negative things about Randy Fine and put in positive things. This appears to be a conflict of interest. I put a warning on Floridagopman's talk page. Anything else that should be done&nbsp;? Thanks <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:RockyMaivia88&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:RockyMaivia88 (page does not exist)">RockyMaivia88</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:RockyMaivia88" title="User talk:RockyMaivia88">talk</a>) 04:36, 6 June 2021 (UTC) </p> <!--
